"\nText\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n|\n\n\n\n52013PC0051\n\nProposal for a COUNCIL REGULATION adapting certain regulations and decisions in the fields of free movement of goods, freedom of movement for persons, company law, competition policy, agriculture, food safety, veterinary and phytosanitary policy, transport policy, energy, taxation, statistics, trans-European networks, judiciary and fundamental rights, justice, freedom and security, environment, customs union, external relations, foreign, security and defence policy and institutions, by reason of the accession of Croatia /* COM/2013/051 final - 2013/0030 (NLE) */\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nEXPLANATORY MEMORANDUM\n1.\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 CONTEXT OF THE PROPOSAL\nThe proposal for a Council Regulation is\nnecessitated by the upcoming accession of the Republic of Croatia to the\nEuropean Union.\nThe Treaty concerning the accession of the\nRepublic of Croatia to the European Union[1]\nwas signed by all Member States of the European Union and the Republic of\nCroatia at Brussels on 9 December 2011.\nArticle 3 (3) of the Treaty of Accession\nprovides that it shall enter into force on 1 July 2013 provided that all the\ninstruments of ratification have been deposited before that date.\nArticle 3(4) of the Treaty of Accession enables\nthe institutions of the Union to adopt before accession measures referred to,\ninter alia, in Article 50 of the Act concerning the conditions of accession of\nthe Republic of Croatia[2].\nThese measures shall enter into force only subject to and on the date of the\nentry into force of the Treaty of Accession.\nArticle 50 of the Act of Accession provides that where acts of the institutions adopted prior to\naccession require adaptation by reason of accession, and the necessary\nadaptations have not been provided for in this Act or its Annexes, the Council\nor the Commission (if the original acts were adopted by the Commission) shall\nadopt the necessary acts. \nPoint 2 of the Final Act[3] refers\nto the political agreement on a set of adaptations to acts adopted by the\ninstitutions which was reached between the Member States and Croatia in the\ncontext of the approval of the Treaty of Accession; the High Contracting\nParties of the Treaty of Accession invited the Council and the Commission to\nadopt these adaptations before accession in accordance with Article 50 of the\nAct of Accession, completed and updated where necessary to take account of the\nevolution of the law of the Union.\nThe present proposal regroups the technical\nadaptations to all Council regulations and decisions as well as to all European\nParliament and Council regulations and decisions which require technical\nadaptation by reason of the accession of Croatia, into a single Council\nregulation.\nAlongside this proposal for a Council\nRegulation, the Commission transmits a series of separate proposals for several\nCouncil directives to the Council which cover technical adaptations to Council\ndirectives as well as to European Parliament and Council directives which also\nneed technical adaptation by reason of the accession of Croatia. Each of these\nseparate proposals for Council directives regroups the technical adaptations\nwhich correspond to different negotiation chapters. This structure is designed\nto facilitate the transposition of the directives by Member States into their\nrespective legal orders, and is in line with the approach which was taken in\nview of the accession of Bulgaria and Romania[4].\nIt is foreseen that all the legal acts included\nin this package will be published in the Official Journal of the European\nUnion at the same date.\nThe present proposal and the other proposals\nincluded in this package will take into account technical adaptations to the acquis\nwhich were published in the Official Journal of the European Union until 1\nSeptember 2012. The reasons for this are to provide sufficient time for the\nlegislative processes involved on the one hand, and for the fulfilment of the ensuing\ntransposition and notification obligations by Member States as regards\ndirectives on the other hand. Adaptations which may be necessary to the acquis\npublished in the Official Journal of the European Union after 1 September 2012\nwill be foreseen in the relevant acts themselves or done at a later stage\nthrough the appropriate procedure. In addition, the\nCommission intends to informally provide a list of such legislation to Member\nStates in early July 2013.\n2.\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 RESULTS OF CONSULTATIONS WITH THE\nINTERESTED PARTIES AND IMPACT ASSESSMENTS\nAs this proposal is of a purely technical\nnature and does not involve any political choices, consultations with\ninterested parties or impact assessments would not have made sense.\n3.\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 LEGAL\nELEMENTS OF THE PROPOSAL\nThe legal basis for the proposal is Article 50\nof the Act concerning the conditions of accession of the Republic of Croatia. \nThe principles of subsidiarity and\nproportionality are fully respected.\nThe action of the Union is necessary under the\nprinciple of subsidiarity (Article 5 (3) TEU) because it concerns technical\nadaptations to legal acts which were adopted by the Union. The proposal\nrespects the principle of proportionality (Article 5 (4) TEU) because it does\nnot go beyond what is necessary to reach the objective pursued.\n4.\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 BUDGETARY\nIMPLICATIONS\nThis proposal has no budgetary\nimplications.\n2013/0030 (NLE)\nProposal for a\nCOUNCIL REGULATION\nadapting certain regulations and decisions\nin the fields of free movement of goods, freedom of movement for persons,\ncompany law, competition policy, agriculture, food safety, veterinary and\nphytosanitary policy, transport policy, energy, taxation, statistics,\ntrans-European networks, judiciary and fundamental rights, justice, freedom and\nsecurity, environment, customs union, external relations, foreign, security and\ndefence policy and institutions, by reason of the accession of Croatia\nTHE COUNCIL OF THE EUROPEAN UNION,\nHaving regard to the Treaty on the\nFunctioning of the European Union,\nHaving regard to the Treaty of Accession of\nthe Republic of Croatia, and in particular Article 3(4) thereof,\nHaving regard to the Act of Accession of\nthe Republic of Croatia, and in particular Article 50 thereof,\nHaving regard to the proposal from the\nCommission,\nWhereas:\n(1)\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 Pursuant to Article 50 of\nthe Act of Accession, where acts of the institutions adopted prior to accession\nrequire adaptation by reason of accession, and the necessary adaptations have\nnot been provided for in the Act of Accession or its Annexes, the Council,\nacting by qualified majority on a proposal from the Commission, shall, to this\nend, adopt the necessary acts, if the original act was not adopted by the\nCommission.\n(2)\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 The Final Act of the\nConference which drew up the Treaty of Accession indicated that the High\nContracting Parties had reached political agreement on a set of adaptations to\nacts adopted by the institutions required by reason of accession and invited\nthe Council and the Commission to adopt these adaptations before accession,\ncompleted and updated where necessary to take account of the evolution of the\nlaw of the Union.\n(3)\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 The following Regulations\nshould therefore be amended accordingly:\n\u2013              \nin the field of the free movement of goods:\nRegulations (EC) No 1907/2006[5],\n(EC) No 1272/2008[6],\n(EC) No 78/2009[7]\nand (EU) No 1007/2011[8],\n\u2013 and directly applicable in all Member States.\nDone at Brussels, EXTERNAL\nRELATIONS\n1.\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 31993\nR 3030: Council Regulation (EEC) No 3030/93 of 12 October 1993 on common\nrules for imports of certain textile products from third countries\n(OJ L 275, 8.11.1993, p. 1):\n(a)          \nThe following paragraph is added to Article 2:\n'11. The release for free circulation in the\nMember State acceding to the European Union on 1 July 2013, namely Croatia, of\ntextile products which are subject to quantitative limits or to surveillance in\nthe Community and which have been shipped before 1 July 2013 and enter the new\nMember State on or after 1 July 2013 shall be subject to presentation of an\nimport authorisation. Such import authorisation shall be granted automatically\nand without quantitative limitation by the competent authorities of the Member State concerned, upon adequate proof, such as the bill of lading, that the products\nhave been shipped before 1 July 2013. \nSuch licences shall be communicated to the\nCommission.'\n(b)         \nThe following paragraph is added to Article 5:\n'The release for free circulation of textile\nproducts sent from the new Member State acceding to the European Union on 1\nJuly 2013 to a destination outside the Community for processing before 1 July\n2013, and re-imported into the same Member State on or after that date, shall\nupon adequate proof, such as the export declaration, not be subject to quantitative\nlimits or import authorisation requirements. The competent authorities of the Member State concerned shall provide information on those imports to the Commission.'\n(c)          \nThe following is inserted in Annex III, Article\n28(6), second
